},\n   377→};\n   378→\n   379→/* This uses a workqueue to avoid various locking ordering issues */\n   380→static void acpi_video_backlight_notify_work(struct work_struct *work)\n   381→{\n   382→\tif (acpi_video_get_backlight_type() != acpi_backlight_video)\n   383→\t\tacpi_video_unregister_backlight();\n   384→}\n   385→\n   386→static int acpi_video_backlight_notify(struct 397→}\n   398→\n   399→/*\n   400→ * Determine which type of backlight interface to use on this system,\n   401→ * First check cmdline, then dmi quirks, then do autodetect.\n   402→ *\n   403→ * The autodetect order is:\n   404→ * 1) Is the acpi-video backlight interface supported ->\n   405→ *  no, use a vendor interface\n   406→ * 2) Is this a win8 \"ready\" BIOS and do we have a native interface ->\n   407→ *  yes, use a native interface\n   408→ * 3) Else use the acpi-video interface\n   409→ *\n   410→ * Arguably the native on win8 check should be done first, but that would\n   411→ * be a behavior change, which may causes issues.\n   412→ */\n   413→enum acpi_backlight_type acpi_video_get_backlight_type(void)\n   414→{\n   415→\tstatic DEFINE_MUTEX(init_mutex);\n   416→\tstatic bool init_done;\n   417→\tstatic long video_caps;\n   418→\n   419→\t/* Parse cmdline, dmi and acpi only once */\n   420→\tmutex_lock(&init_mutex);\n   421→\tif (!init_done) {\n   422→\t\tacpi_video_parse_cmdline();\n   423→\t\tdmi_check_system(video_detect_dmi_table);\n   424→\t\tacpi_walk_namespace(ACPI_TYPE_DEVICE, ACPI_ROOT_OBJECT,\n   425→\t\t\t\t    ACPI_UINT32_MAX, find_video, NULL,\n   426→\t\t\t\t    &video_caps, NULL);\n   427→\t\tINIT_WORK(&backlight_notify_work,\n   428→\t\t\t  acpi_video_backlight_notify_work);\n   429→\t\tbacklight_nb.notifier_call = acpi_video_backlight_notify;\n   430→\t\tbacklight_nb.priority = 0;\n   431→\t\tif (backlight_register_notifier(&backlight_nb) == 0)\n   432→\t\t\tbacklight_notifier_registered = true;\n
